## `dei` (3 tags)

| Tag | Canonical | Note |
|---|---|---|
| `EntityCommonStockSharesOutstanding` | `CommonSharesOutstanding` | A direct match for the number of common shares outstanding for the filing entity. |
| `EntityListingParValuePerShare` | `CommonStockParValue` | Represents the par or stated value per share, which is a direct match. |
| `EntityPublicFloat` | _null_ | Public float is a market capitalization concept not present in the financial statement-focused canonical taxonomy. |
